What a brainless design! I saw only one waiter throughout the whole hot spring area, including the dressing room. No hot spring I've been to before is not so short of waiters. There are also super mosquitoes in the hot spring area, including changing rooms. I really want to leave soon. The overall feeling is that I never want to come again.
